This gives us breakpoints with css accuracy \n        // This width is converted to an integer and look up pushes an image folder name to the populate carousel function\n        var i = 0;\n        var str = $(\".sampleClass\").css(\"width\");\n        var strLength = str.length;\n        var endNum = strLength - 2;\n        var currWidthSub = str.substring(0, endNum);\n        var currWidth = parseInt(currWidthSub);\n        if (currWidth > 990) {\n            // everything bigger than tablet\n            populateCarousel(\"init\");\n        }\n        if ((currWidth <= 990) && (currWidth function that stops us getting multiple resize messages from the browser and just outputs a final singular value\n        // debouncing function from John Hann\n        // http://unscriptable.com/index.php/2009/03/20/debouncing-javascript-methods/\n        var debounce = function (func, threshold, execAsap) {\n            var timeout;\n\n            return function debounced() {\n                var obj = this, args = arguments;\n                function delayed() {\n                    if (!execAsap)\n                        func.apply(obj, args);\n                    timeout = null;\n                };\n\n                if (timeout)\n                    clearTimeout(timeout);\n                else if (execAsap)\n                    func.apply(obj, args);\n\n                timeout = setTimeout(delayed, threshold || 100);\n            };\n        }\n        // smartresize \n        jQuery.fn[sr] = function (fn) { return fn ? this.bind('resize', debounce(fn)) : this.trigger(sr); };\n\n    })(jQuery, 'smartresize');\n\n    $(window).smartresize(function () {\n        // Called on screen resize (tablet or phone rotation) This is so we can catch
